  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_24d3be0a-7a03-4b1a-b416-2dfd2eeb1321'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer4282637598803515766"><b>Book #2 of the Driven Trilogy</b><br/> <br/>What happens when the one person you never expected suddenly happens to be the one you’ll fight the hardest to keep?<br/><br/>Colton stole my heart.   <span id="freeText4282637598803515766" style="display:none"><b>Book #2 of the Driven Trilogy</b><br /> <br />What happens when the one person you never expected suddenly happens to be the one you’ll fight the hardest to keep?<br /><br />Colton stole my heart. He wasn't supposed to, and I sure as hell didn't want him to, but he crashed into my life, ignited feelings within me that I thought had died forever, and fueled a passion that I never knew could exist.<br /> <br />Rylee fell out of that damn storage closet and into my life. Now I don't think I'll ever be the same. She's seen glimpses of the darkness within me, and yet she's still here. Still fighting for me. She is without a doubt the saint, and I am most definitely the sinner.<br /> <br />How is it the one thing neither of us wanted—neither of us anticipated that fateful night—has us fighting so hard to keep?<br /> <br />He steals my breath, stops my heart, and brings me back to life again all in a split second of time. But how can I love a man who won't let me in? Who continually pushes me away to prevent me from seeing the damaged secrets in his past? My heart has fallen, but patience and forgiveness can only go so far.<br /> <br />How can I desire a woman who unnerves me, defies me, and forces me to see that in the deep, black abyss of my soul there's someone worthy of her love? A place and person I swore I'd never be again. Her selfless heart and sexy body deserve so much more than I'll ever be capable of giving her. I know I can't be what she needs, so why can't I just let her go?<br /> <br />We are driven by need and fueled with desire, but is that enough for us to crash into love?</span>

  <span id="freeText3530090253552228640" style="display:none">Doesn't anyone have any original ideas anymore? Is it just me? I kept getting this sense of déjà vu like I read this all before but it's because I have... <br /><br />I'm so sick of the damaged boy always being sexually abused (did anyone else think of Gideon Cross or was it just me?) or the fact that they communicate through song (maybe you thought of Remington Tate?) or it could have been the fact that he had a horrible mom who let him go hungry only to later be adopted by a wealthy couple (but I think it already happened to Christian Grey didn't it?). <br /><br />At the end of the day this story was nothing more than a remix of a remix of an original.</span>

<div id="review_862384876" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/862384876" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/862384876?book_show_action=true">Feb 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer862384876" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12575989591241569265"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393280066i/8686416._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392871624i/8625993.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i> ^^^ my Colton casting... </i><br/><br/>*** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED *** 4.5 stars<br/><br/><strong>I absolutely LOVED this book!!!!</strong> <strong>I was invested in the story from start to finish. My heart was racing, breaking, melting... I was <em>feeling</em> everything!!! <br/><br/>I love Colton. I love Rylee. I love this series. I'm hooked and I can't wait for more!!!</strong><br/><br/>This book captured my heart from the very first page and I was <em>so</em> impressed with the direction that the storyline went in. Honestly, after the huge cliffhanger that the last book left off, I wa</span>
  <span id="freeText12575989591241569265" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393280066i/8686416._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392871624i/8625993.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> ^^^ my Colton casting... </i><br><br>*** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED *** 4.5 stars<br><br><strong>I absolutely LOVED this book!!!!</strong> <strong>I was invested in the story from start to finish. My heart was racing, breaking, melting... I was <em>feeling</em> everything!!! <br><br>I love Colton. I love Rylee. I love this series. I'm hooked and I can't wait for more!!!</strong><br><br>This book captured my heart from the very first page and I was <em>so</em> impressed with the direction that the storyline went in. Honestly, after the huge cliffhanger that the last book left off, I was a little wary because it opened up the potential for the characters to go down a very frustrating path but they basically just turned it right around in a way that made me have <em>so much</em> respect for them both. <br><br>Mistakes were made and there was a lot of heartache but throughout it all, you could <em>always</em> feel how strongly they felt for each other and how badly they were trying to make things work.<br><br>Even though I really liked Driven, it was a bit of a bumpy road for me at first, but I was really blown away by Fueled. It was a very strong book. The story line was captivating and I did <em>not</em> want to put it down!<br><br>Please note that this is the second book in this trilogy and it directly continues the story from the first book. I'm not going to talk about the plot here but I'll just say that this book starts off right where the last one ended but this time, we got to see that devastating scene from Colton's perspective. We got a glimpse into the memories that were haunting him --  <em>"Memories so horrid he vomits with the reappearance of them."</em> -- and my God where they ever <i>heart breaking</i>.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <strong>
      <em>Spiderman. Batman. Superman. Ironman.</em>
    </strong>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>I love love <em>love</em> Colton, but before I talk about him, I want to take a minute to focus on Rylee because she's honestly now one of my favorite book heroines. She was both kind hearted, deeply understanding and incredibly selfless while still remaining a strong woman who wasn't going to be pushed around by anyone. She set her boundaries and held to them. I totally would want to be friends with her. I loved the way she thought and just generally really respected the decisions she made.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"You know you can talk to me… I won't judge or try to fix you, but sometimes just getting it out, getting rid of the hate or shame or whatever is eating you makes it a tad bit more bearable."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Now... about Colton... this guy was a book hero after my own heart. A gorgeous, tortured Alpha bad boy race car driver with a dark past, a reckless side to him, and also a huge heart who was falling in love for the first time in his life. GAHHH!! I LOVED HIM!!! His back story just tore me up and I could see how strong the demons he was fighting were. My heart really went out to him.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"If you look past the gorgeously rough exterior… there's a scared little boy inside that's afraid of love… he's afraid to love someone because he knows that they'll leave..."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>The chemistry between Colton and Rylee was just off-the-charts HOT and their connection was <em>so</em> intense. I swear I spent a good portion of this book just sitting there fanning myself...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Anticipation… Tonight, Rylee, I want you thinking about me all night long. More specifically everything I plan on doing to you later when I have you alone…  Where my tongue is going to lick. Where my fingers are going to grip. Where my mouth is going to taste. Where my cock is going to stroke. How my body is going to worship every incredible inch of yours."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>But while sex scenes were scorching but my favorite part was honestly seeing them open up to each other. Their relationship wasn't always on a smooth path but they both were trying. They went through lot of ups and downs but everything that happened really made sense for the story -- I even found the times when there were miscommunication bearable because I felt like I could understand where they were both coming from at all times. I can't tell you how important this element is to me as a reader. It's the number one thing I look for in a story and even though it sometimes broke my heart, I really enjoyed the journey.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I know we've made a mess of this, Ry, but we can figure this out… We can get us right."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Ohhh and one more gorgeous side to the story was Colton and the kids that Rylee worked with. There's something unbelievably endearing about a bad boy who is amazing with children but when you add in the fact that that bad boy could also identify with the traumatic pasts that these kids had, it just was emotional overload for me. These scenes brought tears to my eyes more than once.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Any guy that makes you cry isn't worth it." </em>
    <br>
    <em>"Maybe if he makes me cry it's because he IS worth it."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>All in all, I really <em>felt</em> this whole story -- I felt the pain, the love, the heart break, and the healing. The last quarter of the book was intense. Suuuuuper intense. There was a lot of drama and yes, the ending was a big cliffhanger. But interestingly, this one didn't bother me too much because it wasn't a relationship cliffhanger. So, even though I'm dying to read the next book and find out what happens next, I'm also ok and really loved the way the whole ending of this book came together.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Time stands still and it feels like we're the only two people in the world. Just a damaged boy and a selfless girl."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Overall, I was <em>so</em> impressed with this book. It kept me connected to the characters the whole way through and I was glued to the page from start to finish. I highly recommend checking this series out! It's fun, addictive, heart felt, emotional... it's got it all!! And best of all -- it has Colton Donavan ;)<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>I want her to own me.</em>
    <br>
    <em>Every fucking piece of me.</em>
    <br>
    <em>Game over baby.</em>
    <br>
    <em>She's my motherfucking checkered flag. </em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><br><strong>Rating: 4.5+ stars</strong><br><br><br><b> MY REVIEW OF BOOK #1: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1dgJMql">http://bit.ly/1dgJMql</a> </b><br><br>****************************<br><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="12575989591241569265" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1150181057" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9395134030141780970"><b>
  <i>5+++++ Spiderman. Batman. Superman. Ironman. Superhero stars.</i>
</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/A98947C2-2BB0-4DBB-B3D5-D9D2E5E2A1EE_zpsquxfgq1k.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437782271i/15628550._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo A98947C2-2BB0-4DBB-B3D5-D9D2E5E2A1EE_zpsquxfgq1k.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/> <br/>What a whirlwind, I read last night till 2am bear in mind I worked till 7pm yesterday too but Colton Donovan is a hero that I just couldn't stand to <b>NOT</b> read any longer. Especially come the 70% I was hooked line and sinker into where it was going. If you EVER read my reviews and recommendations listen here, READ these books they are <b>MASTERPIECES.</b><br/> <br/>Fueled starts up as Driven finishes and in this instalment they are blanketing th</span>
  <span id="freeText9395134030141780970" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>5+++++ Spiderman. Batman. Superman. Ironman. Superhero stars.</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/A98947C2-2BB0-4DBB-B3D5-D9D2E5E2A1EE_zpsquxfgq1k.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437782271i/15628550._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo A98947C2-2BB0-4DBB-B3D5-D9D2E5E2A1EE_zpsquxfgq1k.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>What a whirlwind, I read last night till 2am bear in mind I worked till 7pm yesterday too but Colton Donovan is a hero that I just couldn't stand to <b>NOT</b> read any longer. Especially come the 70% I was hooked line and sinker into where it was going. If you EVER read my reviews and recommendations listen here, READ these books they are <b>MASTERPIECES.</b><br> <br>Fueled starts up as Driven finishes and in this instalment they are blanketing themselves in each other, and entwining who they are within each other. It is a <b>ROLLARCOASTER OF EMOTIONS.</b> I couldn't breathe, I Loved them, hated them, loved Ace, Hated him, was pissed at Rylee, then Felt for her. But in the end I just loved them both just be prepared for the emotions in this one, it takes root in your heart but in a very good way that's all I'm saying. <br> <br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/B9760A4A-8496-47F1-AE82-BAB791019010_zpsvtbojgmx.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438009960i/15655729._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo B9760A4A-8496-47F1-AE82-BAB791019010_zpsvtbojgmx.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><b>Rylee</b><br>What I love about Ryle's is how she doesn't take any bullshit from <b>ANYONE</b> including Ace and how he handles his feelings. But ultimately how she handles the mammoth of attraction and jealousy that comes with him. Yet she knows how to be handled, and won't let others TREAT HER with anything but respect even though she has deep feelings for Colton <b>SHE WILL NOT BE CRUMBLED.</b> <br><br> <a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/5577D62D-FE39-4111-8A49-7314C32F2478_zpsndjzmcn6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438009960i/15655730._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 5577D62D-FE39-4111-8A49-7314C32F2478_zpsndjzmcn6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I love how they balance each other and this story is as much about Rylee as it is about Colton Fucking Donovan. Yet he needs care and unconditional love. I just want-ed to hug him and make it all better, as here we have a boy as much as a <b>MAN</b>, an undercurrent plot that continued to pull at my heart in <b>EVERYWAY</b><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/60FB40CB-D291-492C-A6D4-1A4CB058AAB7_zpsh3n9g6ll.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438009960i/15655731._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 60FB40CB-D291-492C-A6D4-1A4CB058AAB7_zpsh3n9g6ll.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>A SUPERHERO that is Colton Donovan</b><br>I CANNOT put into words how I feel like he has cemented himself and his Rylee into my heart because all in all I AM IN LOVE with them both. I think for the first time I truly love both of these characters, but especially Colton. He is a No 1 hero in sooo many ways, I think these sentences and picture pretty much sums up the kind of man he is. <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/an%20hero_zpss1eidstu.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438009960i/15655732.jpg" alt=" photo an hero_zpss1eidstu.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>A hero that needs love <br>A hero that needs to feel valued.<br>A hero that needs to feel cherished. <br>A hero needs to know that he's not alone. <br>A hero that needs to feel safe. <br>A hero that needs more than predictability. </blockquote>
</b><br><br>I'd say ultimately Ace's vulnerability shines through on this one and you see into his heart and the depth of his soul; that as a reader you want to just grab hold of the pages and feel it <b>ALL</b> right along with him, and hold Rylee's hand to keep strong and keep going. <br><br> <a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/gifs/holding%20each%20other%20gif_zpsfdsyiokf.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438009960ra/15655733.gif" alt=" photo holding each other gif_zpsfdsyiokf.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Onto Crashed&gt;&gt;&gt;&gt;&gt; That. Is. All</b><br><br><b>For more Reviews and Blog posts</b><br><a href="http://slutsistas.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417650623i/12469037._SX540_.png" height="90" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_617951801" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/617951801" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/617951801?book_show_action=true">May 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer617951801" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9988613703041468206"><b>5 not-broken-but-bent-stars<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421956ra/838927.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Sweet Christ. Ladies, get out some tissues and a clean pair of panties because Colton-Mother-Fucking-Donovan is here. And not only is he still pure heat, but his broken is showing. </b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400177ra/775198.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7047863.K__Bromberg' title='K. Bromberg' rel='nofollow noopener'>K. Bromberg</a> delivers an amazing follow up to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17798287.Driven__Driven___1_' title='Driven (Driven, #1) by K. Bromberg' rel='nofollow noopener'>Driven</a>. Colton is still our favorite bad-boy playboy that is every bit alpha-male but we get to see a glimpse into his early years and the events that shaped his life.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>Pleasure to bury the pain.</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>This book took my emotions and just destroyed them</span>
  <span id="freeText9988613703041468206" style="display:none"><b>5 not-broken-but-bent-stars<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421956ra/838927.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sweet Christ. Ladies, get out some tissues and a clean pair of panties because Colton-Mother-Fucking-Donovan is here. And not only is he still pure heat, but his broken is showing. </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400177ra/775198.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7047863.K__Bromberg" title="K. Bromberg" rel="nofollow noopener">K. Bromberg</a> delivers an amazing follow up to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17798287.Driven__Driven___1_" title="Driven (Driven, #1) by K. Bromberg" rel="nofollow noopener">Driven</a>. Colton is still our favorite bad-boy playboy that is every bit alpha-male but we get to see a glimpse into his early years and the events that shaped his life.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Pleasure to bury the pain.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>This book took my emotions and just destroyed them. I was fanning myself one moment and then curled up in a ball in the next. Colton has wormed his way into my heart. I race him, I race the ever-loving-shit out of him. <br><br>As Colton and Rylee navigate through their relationship, one thing keeps coming back to haunt Rylee - the idea that this is all just a simple arrangement, something that has an expiration date. But her heart already belongs to the man that doesn't believe that anything good can ever come of those three words. <br><br>But as Rylee works her way into his system with that damn Voodoo Pussy, it stirs up memories that he has forced down for years. Parts of his life that he has never shared with anyone. The things that were done to him and the things he was forced to do.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I’ve never let someone this far in because that means secrets are shared and pasts are discovered. And because it means you need. I’ve only ever needed myself – needing others only results in pain. In abandonment. In unspeakable horror. And yet, I need Rylee right now.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>We get to see so many different sides to Colton that were hidden from view before. But the part that breaks my heart is the insight into the broken boy. His flashes back to his childhood and his fear of what would come if that is exposed brought me to my knees. With every memory, my heart broke a little bit more for Colton. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Spiderman. Batman. Superman. Ironman.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>This has to be one of the best follow up novels that I have read in a while. Sometimes the middle book can become just a method to pave the way to the conclusion. That is not the case with Fueled. The story went so far beyond just the steamy sheets scenes that we all loved. I had not expected when I came across Driven back in May to find a story that I was going to crave. It was such a pleasant surprise discovering this series and with each book it just keeps getting better. <br><br>But there is one tiny little issue, one little flaw in the perfection that is Fueled. The ending. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/652908.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This was not a standard cliffhanger, this was the mother of all cliffhangers. And although I highly respect that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17880714.Crashed__Driven___3_" title="Crashed (Driven, #3) by K. Bromberg" rel="nofollow noopener">Crashed</a> won't have a release date until it is a firm date, that won't stop me from my begging and pleading like a petulant child for it now. <br><br>For some, knowing that there is a cliffhanger is the reason for waiting for the last book to come out. Although I would love to have the willpower to do this, after sinking my teeth into Driven, there is no way I could have waited to start Fueled. Don't wait to experience this series, we may get left with red swollen eyes from crying, but deep down we know that that their journey just has to lead to a HEA eventually. The road may be paved in painful moments but it will happen. <br><br>Oh, yeah - one last little message to A.C.E:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421956i/838928.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="9988613703041468206" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer8738083463352457531"><b>4,5 “Race You” Stars. </b>	<br/><br/>In this second installment Rylee and Colton have a LOT to figure out after how things ended on the first book. They know their relationship isn’t usual in any way, but they can’t be away from each other. In this book their pasts and Colton’s ghosts keep getting in the way and when their feelings crash and they aren’t capable of hiding them anymore, they’ll know the fight is just getting harder. What neither of them expected it that the biggest fight of all, would be Colton</span>
  <span id="freeText8738083463352457531" style="display:none"><b>4,5 “Race You” Stars. </b>	<br><br>In this second installment Rylee and Colton have a LOT to figure out after how things ended on the first book. They know their relationship isn’t usual in any way, but they can’t be away from each other. In this book their pasts and Colton’s ghosts keep getting in the way and when their feelings crash and they aren’t capable of hiding them anymore, they’ll know the fight is just getting harder. What neither of them expected it that the biggest fight of all, would be Colton himself. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419358180i/13045362.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book was an angsty emotional-rollercoaster. In every five minutes that all seemed to good to be true… it was. The we would have drama, drama, drama. And well, lots of sex. <br>This second installment was WAY better than the first and although not perfect (there was some unnecessary drama trough it), it was a great, raw and emotional reading. The writing was great, additive, and I couldn’t put this book down until I’ve finished it. I seriously don’t understand why it take so much time to read this. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402872274i/10002999.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4,5 Stars<br> <b>Characters Development: </b> I liked Rylee before, but she seriously had me in this one. She is fierce. She is strong and she fights like hell for Colton and she didn’t give up, even when it seemed he was broken behind repair. And Colton, how can we not love the broken man who is clearly out of his zone of comfort? It was nice to finally see him trying to destroy some of its all, and although it’s pretty clear he loves Rylee, he still have a lot to do. 	<br> <b>Steam: </b> Hot. <br> <b>Sensible Subjects: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Abuse. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>Love Triangle: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Well, there is one scene were technically is cheating. But everything is sorted out (almost) after and seriously, don’t let that tiny moment keep you from reading the book.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[MOTHER EFFING CLIFFHANGER! THE MOTHER OF ALL OF THEM! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

I decided to stop reading at 94% (chapter forty) just because I did not want to be like everyone that is now umpatiently waiting for the next book who does not even have a release date to come out. So yes perhaps I don't know what the cliffhanger is this time around but knowing Colton and Rylee? <div id="review_638864435" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/638864435" />
    <a title="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11672704-donna-the-romance-cover"><img alt="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1369044455p2/11672704.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/638864435?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Donna ~ The Romance Cover" href="/user/show/11672704-donna-the-romance-cover">Donna ~ The Romance Cover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer638864435" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11390371706888915929">OMG what have I just read, Kristy Bromberg has hit it out the ball park...review to follow on release....I still can't believe it...so bloody good and so emotional...be prepared....but it is sooooooooooooo good!! Did I say it was good??? I freaking loved loved loved it!!!!<br/><br/>REVIEW!!!!!!!<br/><br/>Fueled – Kristy Bromberg<br/><br/> <br/>5 – emotional and amazeballs stars!!<br/><br/> <br/><b>“Spiderman. Batman. Superman. Ironman.”</b><br/><br/> <br/>K Bromberg has ruined super heroes for me now. I am never, ever going be able to watch these films or cartoons w</span>
  <span id="freeText11390371706888915929" style="display:none">OMG what have I just read, Kristy Bromberg has hit it out the ball park...review to follow on release....I still can't believe it...so bloody good and so emotional...be prepared....but it is sooooooooooooo good!! Did I say it was good??? I freaking loved loved loved it!!!!<br /><br />REVIEW!!!!!!!<br /><br />Fueled – Kristy Bromberg<br /><br /> <br />5 – emotional and amazeballs stars!!<br /><br /> <br /><b>“Spiderman. Batman. Superman. Ironman.”</b><br /><br /> <br />K Bromberg has ruined super heroes for me now. I am never, ever going be able to watch these films or cartoons with my kids again without thinking about Colton Donavan. By the way “I race you Colton Donavan.” I loved him in Driven and I absolutely adore him now….not so much the author, after what she has just put me through!! (she knows I am kidding!!) Seriously though, this book is emotional, very very emotional, I have cried at books before, but this book sent me over the edge so many times. I was convinced I was all cried out and then I would sit back and reflect and the tears would fall all over again.<br /><br /> <br />This book starts with a Prologue that just pulls you in and it is one that starts that emotional rollercoaster from the very beginning, you remember how Driven finished?? Colton chucking Rylee out after saying some very hateful words, well this prologue is recounting the dream that Colton had, that led up to those events and they are not pretty and from Colton’s POV.<br /><br /> <br /><b>“She pushes me.<br /><br />Unmans me.<br /><br />Consumes me.<br /><br />Scares the ever loving shit out of me.”</b><br /><br /> <br />Colton is scared and extremely frightened, the feelings that he has for Rylee are exceptionally alien to him, it has been drilled into him from a young age that only his mother can “love him”, he associates love as a bad thing, in fact a very bad thing and it is something that he feels is a poison to those on the giving and receiving end. This is why he has his “agreements”, if love isn’t involved, there cannot be any poison, he will be safe. As his back story is told through this book it is truly heart breaking, his mother (well a very loose term for such an evil piece of shit), I just wanted to teleport into the kindle and murder her with my bare hands, yes she is THAT BAD!!!<br /><br /> <br /><br /><b>“Good little boys don’t cry if they love their mommies.”</b><br /><br /> <br />It goes a long way in explaining why Colton is the way he is. I thank the lord that he managed to get away and stumble onto the Westin’s doorstep at the ripe old age of 8, what that child had gone through beggars belief and you cannot help but be moved and emotionally invested. Your heart breaks for him, especially if you are a mother, in fact I bet even if you are the most cold hearted of people, his story will touch you in places you never knew existed.<br /><br /> <br />This book is written in dual POV’s which I love, we get to see both Rylee and Colton’s thoughts and feelings. Colton is his usually dominating, alpha self, humorous as ever but as explained above, we see his emotional side, vulnerable side and he really evolves in this book. Whether he wanted to or not Rylee has irrevocably changed him and despite his thinking that he can revert to his old ways when the going gets his tough, he is appalled when he realises that he cannot go back.<br /><br /> <br /><b>“She must have a voodoo pussy or something. Reeling me up and snagging me in her hooks without realizing it.”<br /><br /> <br /><br />“You know, a couple of months ago, I might have answered you differently. But since you fell out of the damn storage closet, nothing has been the same.” He pauses momentarily as he struggles to find his next words, his fingertip trailing down the bare line of my spine. “No one’s mattered before. Ever. But you? F**k, somehow you changed that. You matter.”</b><br /><br /> <br /> <br />Rylee is her usual selfless self in this book, she still has her own issues to contend with as well as Colton’s. It is difficult for her in this book and I did really feel for her at times. I also wanted to slap her so bad in parts, for someone so in the know with regards to broken souls I thought that she could have handled certain things differently, I just wanted to go up to her and say “communicate” for god’s sake “communicate.” I understood her reasoning, she wanted to protect herself, but she was putting herself through needless pain and suffering as well as my poor Colton…yes he is mine so hands off y’all!! She has major insecurity issues in this book, Colton is always surrounded by a bevvy of beauties and she finds it hard to see why Colton wants and needs her. Colton really shines here and always manages to say the right things at the right time. For someone who doesn’t do relationships, he is beginning to learn.<br /><br /> <br /><b>“I want you to see what I see. I want you to see how sexy and desirable and f**king hot you are”, he whispers against the bare skin of my shoulder. “I want you to see what you do to me. How you – in this body that is beautiful inside and out – cause me to come undone. Can unravel me”… “Can reduce me to nothing and build me up all at the same time.”…</b><br /><br /> <br /><br />I highlighted the hell out of this book, there is so much I could add but I don’t want to spoil it for you all. This is a book about their relationship, there are lots of ups and downs, misunderstandings, extremely hot sex but is a journey of discovery for both of them. It is beautiful, it is ugly, it will make you laugh, it will make you cry but it is honest. It is beautifully written, extremely addictive, I could not put it down. I can’t put into words how much I enjoyed this book, although I was emotionally spent by the end, I loved it, I savoured it and I will definitely be reading it again.<br /><br /> <br /><b>“We’re not broken, baby… we’re just bent. And bent’s okay. Bent means we are just figuring things out.”</b><br /><br /> <br />The end…is the end…I was mortified when I read those two little words…don’t ask for clues…I will not say…but all I will add is that I need book 3 NOW!! I seriously cannot wait for book 3…I need book 3. If K Bromberg needs Beta’s I’m there…anything to get this baby sooner rather than later. I have loved this series and Fueled only fuels your appetite for more. K Bromberg has managed to pull me into Colton and Rylee’s little bubble and I do not want to leave.<br /><br /> <br />A few of my favourite quotes that do not give too much away, just humour, sense and more humour!<br /><br /> <br /><b>“Roses are red. Lemons are sour. If you open your legs, I’ll be there in an hour.”<br /><br /> <br /><br />“I think he finally found his lifeline.”<br /><br /> <br /><br />“You can bet your ass that’s one chequered flag I’m definitely claiming.”</b><br /><br /> <br />Totally adore this book, cannot recommend it highly enough, if you haven’t read Driven you need to before starting Fueled, they are a series.<br /><br /> <br />K Bromberg, all I can say is that you have hit it out the ball park with this one. Absolutely brilliant…I have cried whilst writing this review soooo many times. I am emotionally exhausted, but what a ride. You have left me with thoughts and feelings that will never go away and that is very hard to do. High five to you!! I love you and hate you at this moment in time. But it is all good!!<br /><br /> <br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.theromancecover.com">www.theromancecover.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11390371706888915929" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_704475509" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/704475509" />
    <a title="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read"><img alt="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1504717217p2/3068938.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/704475509?book_show_action=true">Aug 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**" href="/user/show/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read">Mirjana **DTR - Down to Read**</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=i-like-your-tats">i-like-your-tats</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=i-m-broken">i-m-broken</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=talk-dirty-to-me">talk-dirty-to-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=whos-the-boss">whos-the-boss</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=athletes">athletes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=too-hot-for-tv">too-hot-for-tv</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=paperbacks">paperbacks</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer704475509" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12499678373923745515"><br/><b>***4.5 I RACE this book hard stars***</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>”We’re not broken baby...we’re just bent. And bent is okay. Bent means that we’re just figuring things out.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/>Talk about a 360 from the first book!! This book….this damn book had my blood racing, adrenaline pumping and heart palpitating throughout the entire angsty ride. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398833094ra/9469977.gif' height='300' width='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I saw the mixed reviews to the first book, hell I HAD mixed feelings about the first book, but I was told over and over again to hold on and push through...it’ll be worth it. Well I</span>
  <span id="freeText12499678373923745515" style="display:none"><br><b>***4.5 I RACE this book hard stars***</b><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>”We’re not broken baby...we’re just bent. And bent is okay. Bent means that we’re just figuring things out.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Talk about a 360 from the first book!! This book….this damn book had my blood racing, adrenaline pumping and heart palpitating throughout the entire angsty ride. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398833094ra/9469977.gif" height="300" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I saw the mixed reviews to the first book, hell I HAD mixed feelings about the first book, but I was told over and over again to hold on and push through...it’ll be worth it. Well I’m here to say…..<b>IT’S WORTH IT!</b> This second book was more focused, flowed better and pulled me deeper into the story from the prologue...the FUCKING PROLOGUE!! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385479949ra/7158786.gif" height="198" width="288" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387143986ra/7539162.gif" height="281" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A lot of the redundancy and circular dialogue was gone. The characters stayed true to their actions. Most of my aggravation from the first book was remedied. Don’t get me wrong, these two still had their stupid moments, but I could understand them more now. I understood Colton’s fear better. His hesitation. His reluctance. And Rylee, well she definitely did a better job grappling with her insecurities. She accepted that she needed to be the strong one in this relationship. She needed to give Colton the nurturing environment and acceptance that he craved in order to begin to address his past. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>”You. <i>This</i>, it scares the shit out of me. I don’t know how to…I don’t know what to do…”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Little by little you watch Colton and Rylee chip away at each other’s walls. Although fears of still being thought of as an “arrangement” filter into Rylee’s thoughts and crossing paths with Colton’s previous hookups unnerve her, she holds on to her resolve to build a relationship with Colton. She rationalizes her insecurities, steps back to look at the bigger picture and draws strength from miniscule yet infinite changes that Colton shows her. Through Colton’s POV, and his actions, we see him slowly start to realize that he’s letting Rylee in, realize that he needs her…that she’s slowly healing him. He still doesn’t believe in a full recovery, but now he sees signs of hope for maybe something more than he’s had so far. Each of them giving pieces of themselves to the other. Scared like hell, but they were trying.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>”Spiderman. Batman. Superman. Ironman.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>I love the way songs were interwoven into this story. Sometimes it’s hard to say what’s on your mind or in your heart and the author uses songs and their lyrics at just the right time to convey the perfect message. It could have been clichéd or overused, but each song was perfectly placed and delivered an extra layer of emotion to the scene. Sometimes a line to a song sums it up perfectly.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381612109ra/5096552.gif" alt="description" height="220" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All this gushing and not 5 stars? Well, unfortunately two of Rylee’s actions hit on my female pet peeves…game playing and unnecessary stubbornness. The first one I could somehow wrap my mind around – it <i>really</i> wasn’t her idea so she’s partially excused, but her stubbornness...UH UH...NO WAY. When your heart is involved it’s hard to think rationally at times, I get that...but give a person a minute to explain if you’re angry about a situation. Be an adult. Don’t run away. Don’t ignore them...especially when they’re begging you for that opportunity to explain. GAH...I’m getting frustrated all over again. <br><br>I’m not going to touch too much on the sexual chemistry between these two in this book. I’ll just say...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405354764ra/10385548.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was a second book I wasn’t expecting. A depth of story I didn’t anticipate. The heartbreak and healing. The fight and surrender. At the beginning of the first book I wasn’t sure what I was in store for, and now after only finishing the second book I already know this series is going to hold a special place for me. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392460046ra/8564114.gif" height="268" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>” I want her to own me.<br> Every fucking piece of me.<br> Game over baby.<br> She's my motherfucking checkered flag.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12499678373923745515" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1980439943" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13311175940639631787">I've read and LOVED K. Bromberg's last 3 new releases, so I decided to go back to the beginning and read the Driven series. Colton seems to be a favored hero, so I needed to see for myself. <br/><br/>Overall, I enjoyed the 1st two books of the series. They're sexy, sometimes sweet, angsty, and well-written. I particularly enjoyed Colton's relationship and interaction with the boys. They were all so sweet. However, there was just a tad too much drama in this book for me. I know he has a troubled past and m</span>
  <span id="freeText13311175940639631787" style="display:none">I've read and LOVED K. Bromberg's last 3 new releases, so I decided to go back to the beginning and read the Driven series. Colton seems to be a favored hero, so I needed to see for myself. <br /><br />Overall, I enjoyed the 1st two books of the series. They're sexy, sometimes sweet, angsty, and well-written. I particularly enjoyed Colton's relationship and interaction with the boys. They were all so sweet. However, there was just a tad too much drama in this book for me. I know he has a troubled past and major issues (his behavior is likely an accurate representation), but I just couldn't... Towards the end of the book with the other woman drama and his decision to lie about what really happened....ummm why? <br /><br />If you're into angst, drama, a complex hero, and caring heroine, I recommend this book. <br /><b>3.5 - 3.75 Stars</b></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer872859262" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10989232752297416784"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400128i/775030._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>4 "Spiderman. Batman. Superman. Ironman. " Stars</b><br/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>“I've never had to work so hard for something I never thought I wanted.” <br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394596908ra/8875677.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>This book...this book was such a ride. There were ups and downs and corners that sneaked up on you. It was an emotional rollercoaster ride that at times frustrated me but had me not wanting to put this down.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>This book picks up right where the first left off. For those of</span>
  <span id="freeText10989232752297416784" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400128i/775030._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>4 "Spiderman. Batman. Superman. Ironman. " Stars</b><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I've never had to work so hard for something I never thought I wanted.” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394596908ra/8875677.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>This book...this book was such a ride. There were ups and downs and corners that sneaked up on you. It was an emotional rollercoaster ride that at times frustrated me but had me not wanting to put this down.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This book picks up right where the first left off. For those of you who have read the first book, you know it ends with one hell of a cliffhanger. So of course I had to find out what happens next and jumped right into this one. Plus, I was very upset with Colton and desperately wanted him to redeem himself. As soon as I started reading, that prologue--which gives an insight into Colton's painful childhood--absolutely hurt and sickened me. My poor Colton. Just from that snippet, Colton's behaviour made a whole of a lot more sense. In fact, this entire book helped me understand him more, which I loved because we got more of Colton's pov in this one.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394597229i/8875688._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>I want her to own me. <br>Every fucking piece of me. <br>Game over baby. <br>She's my motherfucking checkered flag. <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>This book focused more on the demons Colton had to move forward from. My heart hurt for him because in many ways, he is still a scared child because of it. I loved the way Rylee was with him and how she helped him become more willing to open up to her. I hurt deeply for the boy he once was and all he had to go through. It was all just so messed up. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I might not be able to tell you the things you need to hear with the traditional words you need to hear them in, but I swear to God, Rylee, I will try. And if I can't, then I'll show you. I'll show you with everything I have-anything it takes-where your place is in my life”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Because we got more chapters in his pov in this one, I felt like I connected with him more than I did in the first book. I got so angry and confused by him in the first but having his train of thought really helped me get him. I couldn't believe how insecure he could actually be and how worthless he saw himself. Seeing him struggle with his pain that held him captive made me fall for him. Seeing his vulnerable side completely melted me. I ended up really loving Colton in this book, even if he was still very much a jackass in this one. I loved seeing him slowly turn carefree, playful, funny, and happy when he was with Rylee.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394597298i/8875699._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“Fight, Colton! For you. For us. For me. You don't get to pull away from me. You don't get to walk away without a second thought. I matter, Colton. I deserve the same more than you do. What we have is not inconsequential.”<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Rylee I still very much liked, which I was really happy about. Usually in trilogy books like this, the heroine gets on my nerves or frustrates the crap out of me. Rylee did have her moments, but it felt believable to me, not in an over the top annoying way. Rylee has insecurties of her own when it comes to Colton. But I like that she has the strength to try to push down her insecurites. She was strong and stood up for herself when she needed to. She was kind and caring. I loved seeing her interact with the children of "The House". She was bold and usually spoke her mind. For the most part she stayed rational. Yeah, she got confused, a bit scared, and frustrated me a bit, but so did Colton. I still really like her and I think she is perfect for Colton.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394596992ra/8875683.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I race you, Ryles,” he says in a voice that’s implacable and unwavering amidst the swirling chaos.<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>I don't want to give much of the story away because it's best you just read it. This book had it all...scorching hot sex scenes, heartbreaking moments, nail biting angst, intense drama, and sweet moments too. I cried, laughed, panted, and smiled. I feel like I enjoyed this book a bit more than the first. I think that's because I loved Colton more in this one. The ending of this book had me so freaking happy. There was a big breakthrough that warmed my heart. This book also ends with a cliffhanger, but it has nothing to do with the relationship between Colton and Rylee. They are at a happy place when this book ends. But I still can't wait to read the next installment. I hope it's as good or better than this one.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="10989232752297416784" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_617739002" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/617739002" />
    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/617739002?book_show_action=true">May 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer617739002" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14603748089650881007"><b>4.5 Stars </b> <br/><br/>Jointly reviewed for :<a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://totallybookedblog.com/'>http://totallybookedblog.com/</a><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421924i/838831._SX540_.png' width='450' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><br/><b>Jenny: </b> Well, we were left hanging at the end of Driven Book #1 in the Driven Trilogy and to be honest we were a little nervous about what to expect in this second installment weren’t we G? Our concerns were that, being a trilogy, this book could possibly fall in the dreaded <i>“filler”</i> trap, as is the case with some trilogies.<br/><br/>How wrong we were! Fueled is anything but a filler! Fueled is an essential component of this story and it almos</span>
  <span id="freeText14603748089650881007" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars </b> <br><br>Jointly reviewed for :<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://totallybookedblog.com/">http://totallybookedblog.com/</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421924i/838831._SX540_.png" width="450" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><b>Jenny: </b> Well, we were left hanging at the end of Driven Book #1 in the Driven Trilogy and to be honest we were a little nervous about what to expect in this second installment weren’t we G? Our concerns were that, being a trilogy, this book could possibly fall in the dreaded <i>“filler”</i> trap, as is the case with some trilogies.<br><br>How wrong we were! Fueled is anything but a filler! Fueled is an essential component of this story and it almost felt as if Driven was a stepping stone leading us to Fueled. Oh the heat factor is still off the charts and the chemistry between Rylee and Colton is in stratospheric proportions, but this book had so much more, it had substance, secrets were uncovered, it was extremely intense at times, very emotional and an absolute must read! I have to say bravo to K Bromberg because she really took this one to a new level in the trilogy stakes that’s for sure! Fans and new readers alike will devour this one, don’t you think so Gitte?<br><br><b>Gitte:</b> Hell yes Jenny, Fueled was without doubt one of the best sequels in a trilogy I’ve ever read. There’s no filler about it and the writing was brilliant. And yes, Driven was the appetizer to the main course of Fueled. With a tantalizing and much needed dessert to follow still in Crashed.<br><br>I was blown away to tears by the prologue and I just knew we had a great read ahead of us. Fueled had just about everything that keeps you addicted and excitedly reading. It had the passion between Rylee and Colton as well as some real emotional tear jerking moments.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Why get attached to someone that will only leave in the end? To someone who will run the other way when they really know about the truths inside me. The poison that clings to my soul….” </i>
</b>- Colton<br><br>The reveals were truly epic and the cliff hanger. Well…..<br><br>Oh and sigh….Colton…..<br><br><b>
  <i>“Colton kisses like a man drawing his last breath and I am his air. It’s passionate and possessive and provocative.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>Jenny:</b> I was sobbing in the prologue. It really hit a nerve with me. It was extremely intense and a deeply moving introduction and set the scene for what was to be the unraveling of Colton Donavan. The man, the myth and just exactly what this 747 load of baggage he carried around consisted of and I have to say, the way the author handled this story was beautifully done. I can’t fault it.<br><br><b>
  <i>“And it is in this moment, being witness to his agony, I realize there are so many different ways a person can ache. So many definitions I never realized behind a simple word. “</i>
</b><br><br>We got emotion in bucket loads and I fell in love with Colton even more if that’s at all possible, and I felt that Rylee really grew in Fueled, she became stronger and I can only see her coming into her own more and more as the trilogy concludes in Crashed.<br><br><b>
  <i>“There’s so much that I need to explain to you. So much I need to say…so much I should have already said to you.”</i>
</b><br><br>Oh don’t get me wrong. There were times the miscommunication between these two drove me crazy and their unwillingness to bend frustrated me but both these characters have so many issues to deal with and learning to trust, love and depend on another is something they must commit to together and watching it unfold through the pages is gripping!<br><br><b>
  <i>“This is what I do for a living and I missed all of the signs. Love and hurt overriding my training.”</i>
</b><br><br>And did I mention Colton…..swoon…I love him! This troubled, broody, sensual man has stolen my heart.<br><br><b>
  <i>“The image of Colton – so magnificent in body yet conflicted in mind and isolated in emotion…”</i>
</b><br><br><b>Gitte:</b> I fell even more in love with Colton if that was possible too. My heart aches for him, his childhood, the open wounds he still carries and I sympathise with him and understand his behaviour even more now.<br><br><b>
  <i>“You at least deserve someone that’s going to try to be what you need…give you what you want…and I don’t think I’m capable of that.”</i>
</b> - Colton<br><br>Really, for me this was Colton’s book, we got his story and how his past affects his here and now as well as his relationship with the gorgeous Rylee.<br><br>We really did get underneath that hard and controlling exterior which hides a damaged soul and a vulnerability that melts your heart.<br><br><b>
  <i>“She pushes me. Unmans me. Consumes me. Scares the ever – loving shit out of me.”</i>
</b> - Colton<br><br>As for Rylee, she really did do a lot of growing up. She needed to transfer her compassion and understanding from her profession into her personal life in order to understand and heal Colton. Not only that, she needed to realise a few important things about herself and her own past too. Overcome her insecurities and the tragedy which mars her life.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I came back. For you. For me. For who we are when we’re together. For the possibilities of what we can be if you’ll just let me in…” </i>
</b>&lt;?i&gt;– Rylee<br><br><b>Jenny:</b> Fueled really did exceed my expectations. I expected this to be a bit of a romp-fest to be honest but what we got was something so far removed from that scenario. We had questions answered, we witnessed Rylee and Colton grow and understand each other more. Getting into Colton’s head was a revelation. His internal thought processes humoured me and broke me.<br><br>This man has been through so much and you know that Rylee is just the woman to expel his demons and show him love beyond anything he imagined, if he will just let down those walls.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Just listen to me Ry…If you really love him, then keep knocking on that fucking steel gate he has around his heart. If he’s worth it to you, you’ll keep at it.”<br>“The damn thing’s got to give sometime and you’re the only one I think is capable of doing it.”</i>
</b><br><br>I know a lot of readers are mentioning the CH word but I don’t consider the ending to be a cliff-hanger. OMG Yes! It killed me and I let out an audible <i>“bloody hell”</i> at the end but to me if felt like a perfect, heart racing ending and set the scene for Crashed. It had my adrenaline pumping, I was on the edge of my seat, I was cursing the author but…….isn’t that how I’m supposed to feel. This is a trilogy after all and I need to want that third book as much as I do my next breath, and I do. I’d say the author achieved that and more. The ending left me gasping and needing more! Roll on Crashed!!!<br><br><b>Gitte:</b> Fueled gave us a bit of everything we love. Passion, humour, angst and drama. It was so well written and whilst I got annoyed a few times at the misunderstandings and the behaviour it took nothing away from how brilliant a second instalment this is. I already miss Colton like crazy…I am irrevocably in love with this man!!! The cliff – hanger well….just see it as a momentary ‘pit stop’……<br><br><b>
  <i>“I’ve never let someone this far in because that means secrets are shared and pasts are discovered. And because it means you need. I’ve only ever needed myself – needing others only results in pain. In abandonment. In unspeakable horror. And yet, I need Rylee right now.” </i>
</b>– Colton<br><br><i>ARC provided by author in exchange for an honest review </i></span>
  <a data-text-id="14603748089650881007" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer677838997752003491"><b>5 'I race you' stars</b><br/><br/>*<br/><br/><i>
  <b>'My body reacts instinctively to Colton's movements</b>
</i> - <b>
  <u>driven</u>
</b> <i>
  <b>by such unexpected need,</b>
</i> <b>
  <u>fueled</u>
</b><i>
  <b> by such a relentless desire, and</b>
</i> <b>
  <u>crashing</u>
</b> <i>
  <b>into unimaginable possibilities.' ~ Rylee</b>
</i><br/><br/>*<br/><br/>Its been a while now since Ive read this book but Im still <b>NOT</b> able to form coherent thoughts - what is wrong with me you ask - yeah you sure know a certain <b>fucking HOT</b> car racer named <b>COLTON DONAVAN</b> right?! - THATS what is! 'Cause this man turned my brain to mush with all </span>
  <span id="freeText677838997752003491" style="display:none"><b>5 'I race you' stars</b><br /><br />*<br /><br /><i>
  <b>'My body reacts instinctively to Colton's movements</b>
</i> - <b>
  <u>driven</u>
</b> <i>
  <b>by such unexpected need,</b>
</i> <b>
  <u>fueled</u>
</b><i>
  <b> by such a relentless desire, and</b>
</i> <b>
  <u>crashing</u>
</b> <i>
  <b>into unimaginable possibilities.' ~ Rylee</b>
</i><br /><br />*<br /><br />Its been a while now since Ive read this book but Im still <b>NOT</b> able to form coherent thoughts - what is wrong with me you ask - yeah you sure know a certain <b>fucking HOT</b> car racer named <b>COLTON DONAVAN</b> right?! - THATS what is! 'Cause this man turned my brain to mush with all his <b>HOTNESS</b> - like totally useless, good for NOTHING!<br /><br />*<br /><br /><i>
  <b>"I want to feel you on the inside. I want to feel your cum coat me when I fuck you. Want to hear that sound you make when you lose it. And. I. Can't. Wait. Any. Longer," ~ Colton</b>
</i><br /><br />*<br /><br /><br />*fansself*...<b>HOLY SHIT</b>...<b>DAMN HOT</b>...I have to say the wait was <b>so</b> totally worth it - right?! This book is the <b>blast</b>. I think it is even better as the first one. I fell in love with Colton and Rylee all over again. <b>LADIES YOU HAVE TO READ IT</b> - it will blow your fucking mind, thats for sure! <br /><br />*<br /><br /><i>
  <b>'My God. The woman is my fucking kryptonite. How did this happen? How did I let her own me? More importantly und fucking shocking, I want her to own me.<br /> <br />Every fucking piece of me.<br /><br />Game over baby.<br /><br />She's my motherfucking checkered flag.' ~ Colton</b>
</i><br /><br />*<br /><br />Now Im really excited how their story will continue in the final book. Cause <b>you DID it AfuckingGAIN</b> - the end of this book made me cry hard. I wanted to throw my kindle against the wall and punch anybody who crossed my fucking way. I think that is exactly the reaction the author wanted to gain with the ending - *claps hands* well done K.!<br /><br />*<br /><br /><i>
  <b>"I race you, Ryles" ~ Colton</b>
</i><br /><br />*<br /><br />But WHY the fuck do you do this shit? - Dont get me wrong - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/7047863.K__Bromberg" title="K. Bromberg" rel="nofollow noopener">K. Bromberg</a> I love you! - I would read the books anyway!!! - *crys ugly tears* <b>why, why oh why</b>...this shit is totally going to fuck with my head! I so cant wait to read the third and final book - hurry the fuck up...pleeeease ;) Can you give us the release date at least please - Im so desperate here right now...<br /><br /><b>GO RIGHT FUCKING NOW</b> and grab your sexy piece of Colton! <br /><br />_________________________________________<br /><br />08/28/13 - update <br /><br /><b>OH MY FUCKING GOD!!! THE WAIT IS FINALLY OVER!!! ITS LIVE LIVE LIVE! WOOOHOOOOOOOO....YES YES YES!!!! OH BOY IM SO HAPPY RIGHT NOW!!! *happy dance* *jumps up and down* *claps hands*<br /><br />LOVE ME SOME COLTON DONAVAN - Ive been waiting way too long for you!</b><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.de/Fueled-The-Driven-Trilogy-ebook/dp/B00ESJ3S94/ref=sr_1_1?s=digital-text&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1377542985&amp;sr=1-1&amp;keywords=fueled">http://www.amazon.de/Fueled-The-Drive...</a><br /><br />_________________________________________<br /><br />05/17/13<br /><br /><b>OH MY GOD ... HOLY CHRIST ... FUCK YEAH!</b><br /><br />WHAT THE FUCK??? August??? Really??? The wait is going to kill me! I NEED this book like yesterday! Why would you do this to me??? Please please please HURRY UP!<br /><br />_________________________________________<br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/722334949" />

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=damaged-hero-heroine">damaged-hero-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=new-adult-romance">new-adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=march-reads">march-reads</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer722334949" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14291178798008754850">Holy Smoly, what an ending!!! I have just finished this book (at 4am!!) and I am so glad I waited until this trilogy was all written before starting it! I would have been so mad at this cliffhanger if the third book hadn't been written yet!! Needless to say, I will be moving on to the final book; Crashed immediately!<br/><br/>I will keep this review fairly short..all I will say is that I did really enjoy this book, although I found myself frustrated towards the last 30% of the story. Rylee, the heroine be</span>
  <span id="freeText14291178798008754850" style="display:none">Holy Smoly, what an ending!!! I have just finished this book (at 4am!!) and I am so glad I waited until this trilogy was all written before starting it! I would have been so mad at this cliffhanger if the third book hadn't been written yet!! Needless to say, I will be moving on to the final book; Crashed immediately!<br /><br />I will keep this review fairly short..all I will say is that I did really enjoy this book, although I found myself frustrated towards the last 30% of the story. Rylee, the heroine became the focus of most of my frustration and anger. The bottom line is that Colton never once led on that he wasn't a "broken" individual, and that he would be a bad choice to make him boyfriend material. Rylee went into their "relationship" fully aware that he had major baggage, and yet when she revealed some heavy duty feelings to him, and he didn't respond the way she would have hoped..she got all angry,scared and insecure. Granted at one point Colton does something that is not good, but he eventually asked for a chance to explain. I get that she put up walls at first, and didn't want to talk to him; but I felt her resistance lasted for far too long within the story. I started to skim in parts because I was just so frustrated with her and basically the same content for a large part of the book. It had become annoying to see Rylee whine and cry. Then Colton started to lash out too, and it became just too much. So that was my reason for the four stars instead of five.<br /><br />The sex in this book is HOT!! Holy smoly, these two have chemistry beyond what I read in most books! K. Bromberg knows how to create a wonderful sex scene. Colton and Rylee tear up the sheets with passion that explodes as soon as they touch. I devoured their love scenes, and beware to anyone who dared try to interupt my reading while I was absorbing all that carnal, animalistic love romping!! Whew! This book will go down as one of the hottest of 2014 for me!<br /><br />That is all I am going to report at this time. I am eager to get started onto "Crashed"! This series is a definite must read for any readers out there who love a hard core alpha male hero, who is broken on the inside but more than willing to give a relationship a try for the one girl that revs his engine!!! (and I am not talking about the engine in his car!!LOL) </span>
  <a data-text-id="14291178798008754850" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1056225991" class="readable"
